This means out of 100 people , 42 Hindus , 14 Muslims , 7 Christians and 6 ' Others ' will register for vote . 1482 . Open letter to Rahul Gandhi . - Okay , this was long overdue .. . Dear Rahul Gandhi ,. . I am not gonna use nick names to address you coz I can't stoop to the low levels that your fellow politicians have defined . So to begin , firstly this is not a love letter . So don't expect stuff like , ' Oh your dimple is so cute , you should be the PM ' and all that . So man up .... coz this is gonna be some serious shit .. . Your ideology of India being energy , and waves in rivers and high tides and uplifting of boats and going back to women at the CII was just a start . Your fundamental understanding of Indian Mujahideen is appalling . Recently , you also gave a speech to some farmers that there are people coming in flights in huge numbers from abroad every day to Delhi to find jobs and you didn't even tell those poor farmers that you were joking . You then said poverty is a state of mind . Then your ' India is a computer ' default program epic fail took it a little further . Look ... We the citizens of India have had enough now .. . At 43 years of age , you lack the maturity of a 12 year old . Even portraying you as a PM candidate brings so much shame on the country . Your understanding of the constitution or your plans on how to run a Government can force Stand up comedians give up their profession . While Babbar talks about 12 rupee meals , you go feed yourself at the homes of the poor and troll them saying , See .. after all there are \ " FREE LUNCHES\ " in this world . Your academia is as questionable as your work experience . There is nothing much on your resume than your surname and with that you have been toying with our country's future with your mother for so many years now .. . If there's even that tiny bit of patriotism left in you , then leave politics . You can join Rahul Mahajan and come on shows like Comedy Circus . I strongly believe that you have immense potential in this field and you will make a brilliant comedian . You don't need a script , it's inherent in you . Just go and talk and you will have the whole nation laughing and trust me that's more satisfying than anything that you can ever achieve in your life .. . Cheers ,. 1477 . Male 18 years , 2 months 16 days . . This is for the man who is everything behind me . The most respected , loved , adored , wonderful man of my life , in short it's my DAD . Dad you are the world's best dad for me ( 95% dads are world's best dad for their child ) . Although I arrived very late in your life when you had many responsibilities in your head but they never hampered you in loving me . You showered me with whatever you had and still showering your love upon me like rain . You had put a lot of effort in upbringing me . You always fulfilled my every small demand without questioning . Once I heard you were saying to mom , \ " If sometimes meal falls short , even then give full plate to babu , You and I can manage but he should not feel crisis . \ " It touched me dad . You purchased me a laptop even when you were having monetary issues , a Galaxy S Advance , clothes for every occasion and hefty schools fees . I know dad , you were never so rich , but still never denied and managed every minute demand of mine . You always provided me with enough pocket money to sustain for month . I know you have a blind faith on me that's why you never influenced me in taking my decisions about my studies , streams , subjects etc . But dad , I still didn't proved it to you . Dad just bless me for not breaking your faith . And I'll prove it to you one fine day that all your hard work , sheer dedication , perseverance didn't went futile . I still remember the day when you wiped while leaving me in my boarding school when I was at a tender age of 7 years and even now in the mature age of 19 years at the railway station while I was leaving for New Delhi . I almost cried after the train left the platform . Sorry dad , I missed to hug you , coz if we had hugged , you would have not controlled yourself . But I regret now , I should have done that . Dad I know I am always in your prayers , bas aapki Dua lag jaye Insha Allah I'll let you overcome our every problem . My only pray to God is to fulfill your dream and I know your dream is Mine . May God always keep you in a healthy state of mind and soul . Love you Dad and miss you .. . South Campus
